
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ sīlakkhandhavaggapāḷi 9. poṭṭhapādasuttaṃ (DN 9)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{9 Poṭṭhapāda Sutta: About Poṭṭhapāda States of Consciousness 1.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{406.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ me sutaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus have i heard.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Once the Lord was staying at Savatthi, in Jeta’s grove, in Anāthapiṇḍika’s park.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tena kho pana samayena poṭṭhapādo paribbājako samayappavādake tindukācīre ekasālake mallikāya ārāme paṭivasati mahatiyā paribbājakaparisāya saddhiṃ tiṃsamattehi paribbājakasatehi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And at that time the wanderer Poṭṭhapāda was at the debating-hall near the Tinduka tree, in the single-halled park of Queen Mallikā, with a large crowd of about three hundred wanderers.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then the Lord, rising early, took his robe and bowl and went to Sāvatthi for alms.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{407.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho bhagavato etadahosi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But it occurred to him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“atippago kho tāva sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya carituṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘It is too early to go to Sāvatthi for alms.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samayappavādako tindukācīro ekasālako mallikāya ārāmo, yena poṭṭhapādo paribbājako tenupasaṅkameyyan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Suppose I were to go to the debating-hall to see the wanderer Poṭṭhapāda?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho bhagavā yena samayappavādako tindukācīro ekasālako mallikāya ārāmo tenupasaṅkami.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And he did so.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{408.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{3.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tena kho pana samayena poṭṭhapādo paribbājako mahatiyā paribbājakaparisāya saddhiṃ nisinno hoti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{There Poṭṭhapāda was sitting with his crowd of wanderers,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{unnādiniyā uccāsaddamahāsaddāya anekavihitaṃ tiracchānakathaṃ kathentiyā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{all shouting and making a great commotion, indulging in various kinds of unedifying conversation,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathidaṃ - rājakathaṃ corakathaṃ mahāmattakathaṃ senākathaṃ bhayakathaṃ yuddhakathaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{such as about kings, robbers, ministers, armies, dangers, wars,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{annakathaṃ pānakathaṃ vatthakathaṃ sayanakathaṃ mālākathaṃ gandhakathaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{food, drink, clothes, beds, garlands, perfumes,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ñātikathaṃ yānakathaṃ gāmakathaṃ nigamakathaṃ nagarakathaṃ janapadakathaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{relatives, carriages, villages, towns and cities, countries,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{itthikathaṃ sūrakathaṃ visikhākathaṃ kumbhaṭṭhānakathaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{women, heroes, street- and well-gossip,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pubbapetakathaṃ nānattakathaṃ lokakkhāyikaṃ samuddakkhāyikaṃ itibhavābhavakathaṃ iti vā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{talk of the departed, desultory chat, speculations about land and sea, talk of being and non-being.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{409.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{4.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{addasā kho poṭṭhapādo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ; disvāna sakaṃ parisaṃ saṇṭhapesi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But Poṭṭhapāda saw the Lord coming from a distance, and so he called his followers to order, saying:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“appasaddā bhonto hontu, mā bhonto saddamakattha.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Be quiet, gentlemen, don’t make a noise, gentlemen!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ samaṇo gotamo āgacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That ascetic Gotama is coming,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{appasaddakāmo kho so āyasmā appasaddassa vaṇṇavādī.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and he likes quiet and speaks in praise of quiet.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{appeva nāma appasaddaṃ parisaṃ viditvā upasaṅkamitabbaṃ maññeyyā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{If he sees that this company is quiet, he will most likely want to come and visit us.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vutte te paribbājakā tuṇhī ahesuṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{At this the wanderers fell silent.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{410.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{5.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho bhagavā yena poṭṭhapādo paribbājako tenupasaṅkami.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then the Lord came to Poṭṭhapāda,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho poṭṭhapādo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{who said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etu kho, bhante, bhagavā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Come, reverend Lord,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{svāgataṃ, bhante, bhagavato.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{welcome, reverend Lord!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{cirassaṃ kho, bhante, bhagavā imaṃ pariyāyamakāsi, yadidaṃ idhāgamanāya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{At last the reverend Lord has gone out of his way to come here.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nisīdatu, bhante, bhagavā, idaṃ āsanaṃ paññattan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Be seated, Lord, a seat is prepared.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nisīdi bhagavā paññatte āsane.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Lord sat down on the prepared seat,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{poṭṭhapādopi kho paribbājako aññataraṃ nīcaṃ āsanaṃ gahetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and Potthapada took a low stool and sat down to one side.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho poṭṭhapādaṃ paribbājakaṃ bhagavā etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Lord said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kāya nuttha, poṭṭhapāda, etarahi kathāya sannisinnā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, what were you all talking about?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kā ca pana vo antarākathā vippakatā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What conversation have I interrupted?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{411.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{6.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vutte poṭṭhapādo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Poṭṭhapāda replied:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tiṭṭhatesā, bhante, kathā, yāya mayaṃ etarahi kathāya sannisinnā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, never mind the conversation we were having just now,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nesā, bhante, kathā bhagavato dullabhā bhavissati pacchāpi savanāya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{it will not be difficult for the Lord to hear about that later.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{purimāni, bhante, divasāni purimatarāni, nānātitthiyānaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ kotūhalasālāya sannisinnānaṃ sannipatitānaṃ abhisaññānirodhe kathā udapādi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In the past few days, Lord, the discussion among the ascetics and Brahmins of various schools, sitting together and meeting in the debating-hall, has concerned the higher extinction of consciousness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘kathaṃ nu kho, bho, abhisaññānirodho hotī’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘How does the cessation of perception happen?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tatrekacce evamāhaṃsu:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Some said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ahetū appaccayā purisassa saññā uppajjantipi nirujjhantipi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“One’s perceptions arise and cease without cause or condition.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye uppajjanti, saññī tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When they arise, one is conscious,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye nirujjhanti, asaññī tasmiṃ samaye hotī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{when they cease, then one is unconscious.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ittheke abhisaññānirodhaṃ paññapenti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is how they explained it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tamañño evamāha:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But somebody else said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘na kho pana metaṃ, bho, evaṃ bhavissati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“No, that is not how it is.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saññā hi, bho, purisassa attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Perceptions are a person’s self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sā ca kho upetipi apetipi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{which comes and goes.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye upeti, saññī tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When it comes, one is conscious,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye apeti, asaññī tasmiṃ samaye hotī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{when it goes, one is unconscious.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ittheke abhisaññānirodhaṃ paññapenti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is how they explained it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tamañño evamāha:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Another said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘na kho pana metaṃ, bho, evaṃ bhavissati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“That is not how it is.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{santi hi, bho, samaṇabrāhmaṇā mahiddhikā mahānubhāvā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{There are ascetics and Brahmins of great powers, of great influence.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{te imassa purisassa saññaṃ upakaḍḍhantipi apakaḍḍhantipi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They draw down consciousness into a man and withdraw it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye upakaḍḍhanti, saññī tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When they draw it down into him, he is conscious,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye apakaḍḍhanti, asaññī tasmiṃ samaye hotī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{when they withdraw it, he is unconscious.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ittheke abhisaññānirodhaṃ paññapenti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is how they explained it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tamañño evamāha:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And another said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘na kho pana metaṃ, bho, evaṃ bhavissati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“No, that is not how it is.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{santi hi, bho, devatā mahiddhikā mahānubhāvā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{There are deities of great powers, of great influence.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tā imassa purisassa saññaṃ upakaḍḍhantipi apakaḍḍhantipi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They draw down consciousness into a man and withdraw it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye upakaḍḍhanti, saññī tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When they draw it down into him, he is conscious,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ samaye apakaḍḍhanti, asaññī tasmiṃ samaye hotī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{when they withdraw it, he is unconscious.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ittheke abhisaññānirodhaṃ paññapenti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is how they explained it.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tassa mayhaṃ, bhante, bhagavantaṃyeva ārabbha sati udapādi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It was in this connection that I thought of the Lord:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘aho nūna bhagavā, aho nūna sugato, yo imesaṃ dhammānaṃ sukusalo’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Ah, surely, the Blessed Lord, the Well-Farer, he is supremely skilled about these matters!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhagavā, bhante, kusalo, bhagavā pakataññū abhisaññānirodhassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Blessed Lord well understands the higher extinction of consciousness.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kathaṃ nu kho, bhante, abhisaññānirodho hotī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What then, Lord, is this higher extinction of consciousness?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{412.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{7.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tatra, poṭṭhapāda, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā evamāhaṃsu:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘In this matter, Poṭṭhapāda, those ascetics and Brahmins who say}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ahetū appaccayā purisassa saññā uppajjantipi nirujjhantipī’ti, āditova tesaṃ aparaddhaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{one’s perceptions arise and cease without cause or condition are totally wrong.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{taṃ kissa hetu?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Why is that?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sahetū hi, poṭṭhapāda, sappaccayā purisassa saññā uppajjantipi nirujjhantipi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{One’s perceptions arise and cease owing to a cause and conditions.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sikkhā ekā saññā uppajjati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Some perceptions arise through training,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sikkhā ekā saññā nirujjhati”.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and some pass away through training.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{413.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kā ca sikkhā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘What is this training?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhagavā avoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{The Lord said.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“idha, poṭṭhapāda, tathāgato loke uppajjati arahaṃ, sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṃ buddho bhagavā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Potṭhapāda, a Tathāgata arises in this world an Arahant, fully-enlightened Buddha, endowed with wisdom and conduct, Well-Farer, Knower of the worlds, incomparable Trainer of men to be tamed, Teacher of gods and humans, enlightened and blessed.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so imaṃ lokaṃ sadevakaṃ samārakaṃ sabrahmakaṃ sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiṃ pajaṃ sadevamanussaṃ sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā pavedeti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He, having realised it by his own super-knowledge, proclaims this world with its devas, māras and Brahmās, its princes and people.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so dhammaṃ deseti ādikalyāṇaṃ majjhekalyāṇaṃ pariyosānakalyāṇaṃ sātthaṃ sabyañjanaṃ, kevalaparipuṇṇaṃ parisuddhaṃ brahmacariyaṃ pakāseti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He preaches the Dhamma which is lovely in its beginning, lovely in its middle, lovely in its ending, in the spirit and in the letter, and displays the fully-perfected and purified holy life.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{191. (MN2 190-212)}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{41. (MN 2, 41—62)}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ dhammaṃ suṇāti gahapati vā gahapatiputto vā aññatarasmiṃ vā kule paccājāto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘This Dhamma is heard by a householder or a householder’s son, or one reborn in some family or other.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so taṃ dhammaṃ sutvā tathāgate saddhaṃ paṭilabhati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Having heard this Dhamma, he gains faith in the Tathagata.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so tena saddhāpaṭilābhena samannāgato iti paṭisañcikkhati — ‘sambādho gharāvāso rajopatho, abbhokāso pabbajjā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Having gained this faith, he reflects: “The household life is close and dusty, the homeless life is free as air.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nayidaṃ sukaraṃ agāraṃ ajjhāvasatā ekantaparipuṇṇaṃ ekantaparisuddhaṃ saṅkhalikhitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ carituṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is not easy, living the household life, to live the fully-perfected holy life, purified and polished like a conch-shell.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yaṃnūnāhaṃ kesamassuṃ ohāretvā kāsāyāni vatthāni acchādetvā agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajeyyan’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Suppose I were to shave off my hair and beard, don yellow robes and go forth from the household life into homelessness!”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{192.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“so aparena samayena appaṃ vā bhogakkhandhaṃ pahāya mahantaṃ vā bhogakkhandhaṃ pahāya appaṃ vā ñātiparivaṭṭaṃ pahāya mahantaṃ vā ñātiparivaṭṭaṃ pahāya}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{shaves off his hair and beard, dons yellow robes and goes forth into the homeless life.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{193.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\EnglishColumn{42.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And having gone forth, he dwells restrained by the restraint of the rules, persisting in right behaviour,}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{skilled in mindful awareness and content.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{194.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kathañca, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu sīlasampanno hoti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And how, Poṭṭhapāda, is a monk perfected in morality?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idha, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu pāṇātipātaṃ pahāya pāṇātipātā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning the taking of life, he dwells refraining from taking life,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nihitadaṇḍo nihitasattho lajjī dayāpanno sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{without stick or sword, scrupulous, compassionate, trembling for the welfare of all living beings.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{(MN 1,8—27)}}\\

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\EnglishColumn{1.8.}}\\

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“adinnādānaṃ pahāya adinnādānā paṭivirato hoti dinnādāyī dinnapāṭikaṅkhī, athenena sucibhūtena attanā viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Abandoning the taking of what is not given, he dwells refraining from taking what is not given, living purely, accepting what is given, awaiting what is given, without stealing.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning unchastity, he lives far from it, aloof from the village-practice of sex.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\

\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saccavādī saccasandho theto paccayiko avisaṃvādako lokassa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{a truth-speaker, one to be relied on, trustworthy, dependable, not a deceiver of the world.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“pisuṇaṃ vācaṃ pahāya pisuṇāya vācāya paṭivirato hoti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning malicious speech,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ito sutvā na amutra akkhātā imesaṃ bhedāya;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he does not repeat there what he has heard here to the detriment of these,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or repeat here what he has heard there to the detriment of those.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti bhinnānaṃ vā sandhātā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is a reconciler of those at variance}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sahitānaṃ vā anuppadātā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and an encourager of those at one,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{samaggārāmo samaggarato samagganandī samaggakaraṇiṃ vācaṃ bhāsitā hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{rejoicing in peace, loving it, delighting in it, one who speaks up for peace.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{porī bahujanakantā bahujanamanāpā tathārūpiṃ vācaṃ bhāsitā hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{urbane, pleasing and attractive to the multitude.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in

\end{addmargin}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He is a speaker whose words are to be treasured,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“bījagāmabhūtagāmasamārambhā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“‘He is a refrainer from damaging seeds and crops.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ekabhattiko hoti rattūparato virato vikālabhojanā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He eats once a day and not at night, refraining from eating at improper times.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{naccagītavāditavisūkadassanā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He avoids watching dancing, singing, music and shows.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mālāgandhavilepanadhāraṇamaṇḍanavibhūsanaṭṭhānā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He abstains from using garlands, perfumes, cosmetics, ornaments and adornments.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{uccāsayanamahāsayanā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He avoids using high or wide beds.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{jātarūparajatapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He avoids accepting gold and silver.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{āmakadhaññapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}

\end{addmargin}

\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kiṃ tvaṃ imaṃ dhammavinayaṃ ājānissasi,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘How could you understand this doctrine and discipline?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{micchā paṭipanno tvamasi, ahamasmi sammā paṭipanno,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Your way is all wrong — mine is right!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sahitaṃ me, asahitaṃ te,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘I am consistent - you aren’t!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pure vacanīyaṃ pacchā avaca, pacchā vacanīyaṃ pure avaca,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘You said last what you should have said first, and you said first what you should have said last!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{adhiciṇṇaṃ te viparāvattaṃ, āropito te vādo,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘What you took so long to think up has been refuted!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{niggahito tvamasi, cara vādappamokkhāya,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Your argument has been overthrown, you’re defeated!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nibbeṭhehi vā sace pahosīti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Go on, save your doctrine — get out of that if you can!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti vā iti evarūpāya viggāhikakathāya paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he refrains from such disputation.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{203.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{1.19.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yathā vā paneke bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā saddhādeyyāni bhojanāni bhuñjitvā te evarūpaṃ dūteyyapahiṇagamanānuyogaṃ anuyuttā viharanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“‘Whereas some ascetics and Brahmins, feeding on the food of the faithful, remain addicted to such things as running errands and messages,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathidaṃ — raññaṃ, rājamahāmattānaṃ, khattiyānaṃ, brāhmaṇānaṃ, gahapatikānaṃ, kumārānaṃ —}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{such as for kings, ministers, nobles, Brahmins, householders and young men who say:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘idha gaccha, amutrāgaccha,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Go here — go there!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idaṃ hara, amutra idaṃ āharā’ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Take this there — bring that from there!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti vā iti evarūpā dūteyyapahiṇagamanānuyogā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he refrains from such errand-running.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{204.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{1.20.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yathā vā paneke bhonto samaṇabrāhmaṇā saddhādeyyāni bhojanāni bhuñjitvā te kuhakā ca honti lapakā ca nemittikā ca nippesikā ca lābhena lābhaṃ nijigīṃsitāro ca. iti evarūpā kuhanalapanā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“‘Whereas some ascetics and Brahmins, feeding on the food of the faithful, remain addicted to deception, patter, hinting, belittling, and are always .on the make for further gains, he refrains from such deception.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{rat-lore, bird-lore, crow-lore, foretelling a person’s life-span, charms against arrows, knowledge of animals’ cries,}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathidaṃ — suvuṭṭhikā bhavissati, dubbuṭṭhikā bhavissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{such as predicting good or bad rainfall;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{subhikkhaṃ bhavissati, dubbhikkhaṃ bhavissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{a good or bad harvest;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{khemaṃ bhavissati, bhayaṃ bhavissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{security, danger;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{rogo bhavissati, ārogyaṃ bhavissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{disease, health;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{muddā, gaṇanā, saṅkhānaṃ, kāveyyaṃ, lokāyataṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or accounting, computing, calculating, poetic composition, philosophising,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti vā iti evarūpāya tiracchānavijjāya micchājīvā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he refrains from such base arts and wrong means of livelihood.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idampissa hoti sīlasmiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Thus he is accomplished in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathidaṃ — āvāhanaṃ vivāhanaṃ saṃvaraṇaṃ vivaraṇaṃ saṅkiraṇaṃ vikiraṇaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{[declaring the time for] saving and spending, bringing good or bad luck, procuring abortions, using spells to bind the tongue, binding the jaw,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{hatthābhijappanaṃ hanujappanaṃ kaṇṇajappanaṃ ādāsapañhaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{making the hands jerk, causing deafness, getting answers with a mirror,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kumārikapañhaṃ devapañhaṃ ādiccupaṭṭhānaṃ mahatupaṭṭhānaṃ abbhujjalanaṃ sirivhāyanaṃ}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{a girl-medium, a deva; worshipping the sun or Great Brahma, breathing fire, invoking the goddess of luck,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti vā iti evarūpāya tiracchānavijjāya micchājīvā paṭivirato hoti.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sa kho so, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu evaṃ sīlasampanno na kutoci bhayaṃ samanupassati, yadidaṃ sīlasaṃvarato.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And then, Poṭṭhapāda, that monk who is perfected in morality sees no danger from any side owing to his being restrained by morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi — poṭṭhapāda, rājā khattiyo muddhābhisitto nihatapaccāmitto na kutoci bhayaṃ samanupassati, yadidaṃ paccatthikato; evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu evaṃ sīlasampanno na kutoci bhayaṃ samanupassati, yadidaṃ sīlasaṃvarato.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Just as a duly-anointed Khattiya king, having conquered his enemies, by that very fact sees no danger from any side, so the monk, on account of his morality, sees no danger anywhere.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so iminā ariyena sīlakkhandhena samannāgato ajjhattaṃ anavajjasukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedeti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He experiences in himself the blameless bliss that comes from maintaining this Ariyan morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu sīlasampanno hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way, Poṭṭhapāda, he is perfected in morality.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{213.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kathañca, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu indriyesu guttadvāro hoti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And how, Poṭṭhapāda, is he a guardian of the sense-doors?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idha, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṃ disvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here a monk, on seeing a visible object with the eye, does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yatvādhikaraṇamenaṃ cakkhundriyaṃ asaṃvutaṃ viharantaṃ abhijjhā domanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because greed and sorrow, evil unskilled states, would overwhelm him if he dwelt leaving this eye-faculty unguarded,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa saṃvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati cakkhundriyaṃ, cakkhundriye saṃvaraṃ āpajjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so he practises guarding it, he protects the eye-faculty, develops restraint of the eye-faculty.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sotena saddaṃ sutvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{On hearing a sound with the ear, does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yatvādhikaraṇamenaṃ sotindriyaṃ asaṃvutaṃ viharantaṃ abhijjhā domanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because greed and sorrow, evil unskilled states, would overwhelm him if he dwelt leaving this ear-faculty unguarded,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa saṃvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati sotindriyaṃ, sotindriye saṃvaraṃ āpajjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so he practises guarding it, he protects the ear-faculty, develops restraint of the ear-faculty.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ghānena gandhaṃ ghāyitvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{On smelling an odour with the nose, does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yatvādhikaraṇamenaṃ ghānindriyaṃ asaṃvutaṃ viharantaṃ abhijjhā domanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because greed and sorrow, evil unskilled states, would overwhelm him if he dwelt leaving this nose-faculty unguarded,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa saṃvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati ghānindriyaṃ, ghānindriye saṃvaraṃ āpajjati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{so he practises guarding it, he protects the nose-faculty, develops restraint of the nose-faculty.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{jivhāya rasaṃ sāyitvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{On tasting a flavour with the tongue, does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yatvādhikaraṇamenaṃ jivhindriyaṃ asaṃvutaṃ viharantaṃ abhijjhā domanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because greed and sorrow, evil unskilled states, would overwhelm him if he dwelt leaving this tongue-faculty unguarded,}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.5}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusitvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.}}\\

{\EnglishColumn{On feeling an object with the body, does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{On thinking a thought with the mind, he does not grasp at its major signs or secondary characteristics.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because greed and sorrow, evil unskilled states, would overwhelm him if he dwelt leaving this mind-faculty unguarded,}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kathañca, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu satisampajaññena samannāgato hoti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And how, Poṭṭhapāda, is a monk accomplished in mindfulness and clear awareness?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idha, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu abhikkante paṭikkante sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here a monk acts with clear awareness in going forth and back,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ālokite vilokite sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in looking ahead or behind him,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{samiñjite pasārite sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in bending and stretching,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saṅghāṭipattacīvaradhāraṇe sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in wearing his outer and inner robe and carrying his bowl,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{asite pīte khāyite sāyite sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in eating, drinking, chewing and swallowing,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{uccārapassāvakamme sampajānakārī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in evacuating and urinating,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{gate ṭhite nisinne sutte jāgarite bhāsite tuṇhībhāve sampajānakārī hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{in walking, standing, sitting, lying down, in waking, in speaking and in keeping silent he acts with clear awareness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu satisampajaññena samannāgato hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way, a monk is accomplished in mindfulness and clear awareness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{215.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{66.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kathañca, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu santuṭṭho hoti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And how is a monk contented?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idha, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu santuṭṭho hoti kāyaparihārikena cīvarena,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here, a monk is satisfied with a robe to protect his body,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kucchiparihārikena piṇḍapātena.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with alms to satisfy his stomach,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so yena yeneva pakkamati, samādāyeva pakkamati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and having accepted sufficient, he goes on his way.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, pakkhī sakuṇo yena yeneva ḍeti, sapattabhārova ḍeti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Just as a bird with wings flies hither and thither, burdened by nothing but its wings, so he is satisfied.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu santuṭṭho hoti kāyaparihārikena cīvarena}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way, a monk is satisfied with a robe to protect his body,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{kucchiparihārikena piṇḍapātena.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with alms to satisfy his stomach,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so yena yeneva pakkamati, samādāyeva pakkamati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and having accepted sufficient, he goes on his way.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu santuṭṭho hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way, Poṭṭhapāda, a monk is contented.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{216.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{67.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“so iminā ca ariyena sīlakkhandhena samannāgato,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Then he, equipped with this Ariyan morality,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iminā ca ariyena indriyasaṃvarena samannāgato,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with this Ariyan restraint of the senses,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iminā ca ariyena satisampajaññena samannāgato,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with this Ariyan mindfulness and awareness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imāya ca ariyāya santuṭṭhiyā samannāgato,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with this Ariyan contentment,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vivittaṃ senāsanaṃ bhajati araññaṃ rukkhamūlaṃ pabbataṃ kandaraṃ giriguhaṃ susānaṃ vanapatthaṃ abbhokāsaṃ palālapuñjaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{finds a solitary lodging, at the root of a forest tree, in a mountain cave or gorge, a charnel-ground, a jungle-thicket, or in the open air on a heap of straw.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātappaṭikkanto nisīdati pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then, having eaten after his return from the alms-round, he sits down cross-legged, holding his body erect, and concentrates on keeping mindfulness established before him.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{217.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{68.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“so abhijjhaṃ loke pahāya vigatābhijjhena cetasā viharati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Abandoning worldly desires, he dwells with a mind freed from worldly desires,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{abhijjhāya cittaṃ parisodheti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and his mind is purified of worldly desire.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{byāpādapadosaṃ pahāya abyāpannacitto viharati}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning ill-will and hatred, he dwells with a mind freed from ill-will and hatred,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī, byāpādapadosā cittaṃ parisodheti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and by compassionate love for the welfare of all living beings, his mind is purified of ill-will and hatred.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{thinamiddhaṃ pahāya vigatathinamiddho viharati}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning sloth-and-torpor, he dwells with a mind freed from sloth-and-torpor,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ālokasaññī, sato sampajāno, thinamiddhā cittaṃ parisodheti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{perceiving light, mindful and clearly aware, his mind is purified of sloth-and-torpor.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{uddhaccakukkuccaṃ pahāya anuddhato viharati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning worry-and-flurry, he dwells with a mind freed from worry-and-flurry,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ajjhattaṃ vūpasantacitto, uddhaccakukkuccā cittaṃ parisodheti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and with an inwardly calmed mind his heart is purified of worry-and-flurry.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vicikicchaṃ pahāya tiṇṇavicikiccho viharati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Abandoning doubt, he dwells with doubt left behind,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{akathaṃkathī kusalesu dhammesu, vicikicchāya cittaṃ parisodheti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{without uncertainty as to what things are wholesome, his mind is purified of doubt.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{218.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{69.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, puriso iṇaṃ ādāya kammante payojeyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Just as a man who had taken a loan to develop his business,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa te kammantā samijjheyyuṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and whose efforts were successful,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so yāni ca porāṇāni iṇamūlāni, tāni ca byantiṃ kareyya, siyā cassa uttariṃ avasiṭṭhaṃ dārabharaṇāya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{might pay off his old debts, and with what was left over could support a wife,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa evamassa — ‘ahaṃ kho pubbe iṇaṃ ādāya kammante payojesiṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{might think: “Before this I developed my business by borrowing,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa me te kammantā samijjhiṃsu.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and those efforts were successful,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sohaṃ yāni ca porāṇāni iṇamūlāni, tāni ca byantiṃ akāsiṃ, atthi ca me uttariṃ avasiṭṭhaṃ dārabharaṇāyā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{paid off old debts, and with what was left over could support a wife.”,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so tatonidānaṃ labhetha pāmojjaṃ, adhigaccheyya somanassaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and he would rejoice and be glad about that.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{219.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{70.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, puriso ābādhiko assa dukkhito bāḷhagilāno;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Just as a man who was ill, suffering, terribly sick,}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and regain his appetite and bodily strength,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{somhi etarahi tamhā ābādhā mutto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{might after a time recover,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhattañca me chādeti, atthi ca me kāye balamattā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and regain his appetite and bodily strength.”,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so tatonidānaṃ labhetha pāmojjaṃ, adhigaccheyya somanassaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{220.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{71.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, puriso bandhanāgāre baddho assa.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He might think: “Before this I was in prison,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{somhi etarahi tamhā bandhanāgārā mutto sotthinā abbhayena.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and after a time I was freed from bonds without any loss,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{natthi ca me kiñci bhogānaṃ vayo’ti.}}\\

\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{with no deduction from my possessions.”,}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{223.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{74.}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu yathā iṇaṃ yathā rogaṃ yathā bandhanāgāraṃ yathā dāsabyaṃ yathā kantāraddhānamaggaṃ, evaṃ ime pañca nīvaraṇe appahīne attani samanupassati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘As long, Poṭṭhapāda, as a monk does not perceive the disappearance of the five hindrances in himself, he feels as if in debt, in sickness, in bonds, in slavery, on a desert journey.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{224.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, yathā āṇaṇyaṃ yathā ārogyaṃ yathā bandhanāmokkhaṃ yathā bhujissaṃ yathā khemantabhūmiṃ; evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu ime pañca nīvaraṇe pahīne attani samanupassati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But when he perceives the disappearance of the five hindrances in himself, it is as if he were freed from debt, from sickness, from bonds, from slavery, from the perils of the desert.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{75.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tassime pañcanīvaraṇe pahīne attani samanupassato pāmojjaṃ jāyati, pamuditassa pīti jāyati, pītimanassa kāyo passambhati, passaddhakāyo sukhaṃ vedeti, sukhino cittaṃ samādhiyati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And when he knows that these five hindrances have left him, gladness arises in him, from gladness comes delight, from the delight in his mind his body is tranquillised, with a tranquil body he feels joy, and with joy his mind is concentrated.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so vivicceva kāmehi, vivicca akusalehi dhammehi, savitakkaṃ savicāraṃ vivekajaṃ pītisukhaṃ paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ upasampajja viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Being thus detached from sense-desires, detached from unwholesome states, he enters and remains in the first jhāna, which is with thinking and pondering, born of detachment, filled with delight and joy.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa yā purimā kāmasaññā, sā nirujjhati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And whatever sensations of lust that he previously had disappear.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vivekajapītisukhasukhumasaccasaññā tasmiṃ samaye hoti, vivekajapītisukhasukhuma-saccasaññīyeva tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{At that time there is present a true but subtle perception of delight and happiness, born of detachment, and he becomes one who is conscious of this delight and happiness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evampi sikkhā ekā saññā uppajjati, sikkhā ekā saññā nirujjhati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way some perceptions arise through training, and some pass away through training.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ sikkhā”ti bhagavā avoca.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And this is that training’, said the Lord.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{11.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“puna caparaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu vitakkavicārānaṃ vūpasamā ajjhattaṃ sampasādanaṃ cetaso ekodibhāvaṃ avitakkaṃ avicāraṃ samādhijaṃ pītisukhaṃ dutiyaṃ jhānaṃ upasampajja viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Again, a monk, with the subsiding of thinking and pondering, by gaining inner tranquillity and unity of mind, reaches and remains in the second jhāna, which is free from thinking and pondering, born of concentration, filled with delight and happiness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa yā purimā vivekajapītisukhasukhumasaccasaññā, sā nirujjhati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{His former true but subtle perception of delight and happiness born of detachment vanishes.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{samādhijapītisukhasukhumasaccasaññā tasmiṃ samaye hoti, samādhijapītisukhasukhumasaccasaññīyeva tasmiṃ samaye hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{At that time there arises a true but subtle perception of delight and happiness born of concentration, and he becomes one who is conscious of this delight and happiness.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evampi sikkhā ekā saññā uppajjati, sikkhā ekā saññā nirujjhati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{12.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“puna caparaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu pītiyā ca virāgā upekkhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno, sukhañca kāyena paṭisaṃvedeti, yaṃ taṃ ariyā ācikkhanti:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Again, after the fading away of delight he dwells in equanimity, mindful and clearly aware, and he experiences in his body that pleasant feeling of which the Noble Ones say:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Happy dwells the man of equanimity and mindfulness”, and he reaches and remains in the third jhāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and there arises at that time a true but subtle sense of equanimity and happiness, and he becomes one who is conscious of this true but subtle sense of equanimity and happiness.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{“puna caparaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānaṃ atthaṅgamā adukkhamasukhaṃ upekkhāsatipārisuddhiṃ catutthaṃ jhānaṃ upasampajja viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\EnglishColumn{14.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“puna caparaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu sabbaso rūpasaññānaṃ samatikkamā paṭighasaññānaṃ atthaṅgamā nānattasaññānaṃ amanasikārā ‘ananto ākāso’ti ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ upasampajja viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Again, by passing entirely beyond bodily sensations, by the disappearance of all sense of resistance and by non-attraction to the perception of diversity, seeing that space is boundless, he reaches and remains in the sphere of boundless space.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\PaliColumn{“puna caparaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu sabbaso viññāṇañcāyatanaṃ samatikkamma ‘natthi kiñcī’ti ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ upasampajja viharati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
