\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And this is that training’, said the Lord.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{414.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{17.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yato kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu idha sakasaññī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Potthapada, from the moment when a monk has gained this controlled perception,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so tato amutra tato amutra anupubbena saññaggaṃ phusati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he proceeds from stage to stage till he reaches the limit of perception.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa saññagge ṭhitassa evaṃ hoti:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When he has reached the limit of perception it occurs to him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘cetayamānassa me pāpiyo, acetayamānassa me seyyo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Mental activity is worse for me, lack of mental activity is better.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ahañceva kho pana ceteyyaṃ, abhisaṅkhareyyaṃ, imā ca me saññā nirujjheyyuṃ, aññā ca oḷārikā saññā uppajjeyyuṃ;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{If I were to think and imagine, these perceptions [that I have attained] would cease, and coarser perceptions would arise in me.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yaṃnūnāhaṃ na ceva ceteyyaṃ na ca abhisaṅkhareyyan’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Suppose I were not to think or imagine?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so na ceva ceteti, na ca abhisaṅkharoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So he neither thinks nor imagines.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa acetayato anabhisaṅkharoto tā ceva saññā nirujjhanti, aññā ca oḷārikā saññā na uppajjanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And then, in him, just these perceptions arise, but other, coarser perceptions do not arise.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so nirodhaṃ phusati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He attains cessation.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho, poṭṭhapāda, anupubbābhisaññānirodha-sampajāna-samāpatti hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And that, Poṭṭhapāda, is the way in which the cessation of perception is brought about by successive steps.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{18.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ kiṃ maññasi, poṭṭhapāda,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘What do you think, Poṭṭhapāda?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{api nu te ito pubbe evarūpā anupubbābhisaññānirodha-sampajāna-samāpatti sutapubbā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Have you heard of this before?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“no hetaṃ, bhante.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘No, Lord.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho ahaṃ, bhante, bhagavato bhāsitaṃ ājānāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{As I understand it, the Lord has said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘yato kho, poṭṭhapāda, bhikkhu idha sakasaññī hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Poṭṭhapāda, from the moment when a monk has gained this controlled perception,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so tato amutra tato amutra anupubbena saññaggaṃ phusati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{he proceeds from stage to stage till he reaches the limit of perception.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa saññagge ṭhitassa evaṃ hoti:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{When he has reached the limit of perception it occurs to him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“cetayamānassa me pāpiyo, acetayamānassa me seyyo.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Mental activity is worse for me, lack of mental activity is better.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ahañceva kho pana ceteyyaṃ abhisaṅkhareyyaṃ, imā ca me saññā nirujjheyyuṃ, aññā ca oḷārikā saññā uppajjeyyuṃ;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{If I were to think and imagine, these perceptions [that I have attained] would cease, and coarser perceptions would arise in me.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yaṃnūnāhaṃ na ceva ceteyyaṃ, na ca abhisaṅkhareyyan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Suppose I were not to think or imagine?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so na ceva ceteti, na cābhisaṅkharoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{So he neither thinks nor imagines.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tassa acetayato anabhisaṅkharoto tā ceva saññā nirujjhanti, aññā ca oḷārikā saññā na uppajjanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And then, in him, just these perceptions arise, but other, coarser perceptions do not arise.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so nirodhaṃ phusati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{He attains cessation.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho, poṭṭhapāda, anupubbābhisaññānirodha-sampajāna-samāpatti hotī’”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And that, Poṭṭhapāda, is the way in which the cessation of perception is brought about by successive steps.”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evaṃ, poṭṭhapādā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘That is right, Poṭṭhapāda.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{415.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{19.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekaññeva nu kho, bhante, bhagavā saññaggaṃ paññapeti, udāhu puthūpi saññagge paññapetī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, do you teach that the summit of perception is just one, or that it is many?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekampi kho ahaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, saññaggaṃ paññapemi, puthūpi saññagge paññapemī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘I teach it as both one and many.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yathā kathaṃ pana, bhante, bhagavā ekampi saññaggaṃ paññapeti, puthūpi saññagge paññapetī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, how is it one, and how is it many?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yathā yathā kho, poṭṭhapāda, nirodhaṃ phusati, tathā tathāhaṃ saññaggaṃ paññapemi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘According as he attains successively to the cessation of each perception, so I teach the summit of that perception:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ kho ahaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, ekampi saññaggaṃ paññapemi, puthūpi saññagge paññapemī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{thus I teach both one summit of perception, and I also teach many.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{416.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{20.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“saññā nu kho, bhante, paṭhamaṃ uppajjati, pacchā ñāṇaṃ, udāhu ñāṇaṃ paṭhamaṃ uppajjati, pacchā saññā, udāhu saññā ca ñāṇañca apubbaṃ acarimaṃ uppajjantī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, does perception arise before knowledge, or knowledge arise before perception, or do both arise simultaneously?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“saññā kho, poṭṭhapāda, paṭhamaṃ uppajjati, pacchā ñāṇaṃ, saññuppādā ca pana ñāṇuppādo hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{’ ‘Perception arises first, Poṭṭhapāda, then knowledge, and from the arising of perception comes the arising of knowledge.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so evaṃ pajānāti:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And one knows:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘idappaccayā kira me ñāṇaṃ udapādī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Thus conditioned, knowledge arises.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iminā kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way you can see how}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yathā saññā paṭhamaṃ uppajjati, pacchā ñāṇaṃ, saññuppādā ca pana ñāṇuppādo hotī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{perception arises first, and then knowledge, and that from the arising of perception comes the arising of knowledge.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{417.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“saññā nu kho, bhante, purisassa attā, udāhu aññā saññā añño attā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, is perception a person’s self, or is perception one thing, and self another?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kaṃ pana tvaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, attānaṃ paccesī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Poṭṭhapāda, do you postulate a self?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“oḷārikaṃ kho ahaṃ, bhante, attānaṃ paccemi rūpiṃ cātumahābhūtikaṃ kabaḷīkārāhārabhakkhan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, I postulate a gross self, material, composed of the four elements, and feeding on solid food.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“oḷāriko ca hi te, poṭṭhapāda, attā abhavissa rūpī cātumahābhūtiko kabaḷīkārāhārabhakkho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But with such a gross self, Poṭṭhapāda, composed of the four elements, and feeding on solid food.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ santaṃ kho te, poṭṭhapāda, aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In that case, perception would be one thing, and the self another.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tadamināpetaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here is another way to understand how perception and self are different things.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tiṭṭhateva sāyaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, oḷāriko attā rūpī cātumahābhūtiko kabaḷīkārāhārabhakkho,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{As long as that gross self persists, composed of the four elements, and feeding on solid food,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha imassa purisassa aññā ca saññā uppajjanti, aññā ca saññā nirujjhanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{certain perceptions would arise in a person, and others pass away.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iminā kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way you can see that perception must be one thing, the self another.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{418.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“manomayaṃ kho ahaṃ, bhante, attānaṃ paccemi sabbaṅgapaccaṅgiṃ ahīnindriyan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, I postulate a mind-made self complete with all its parts, not defective in any sense-organ.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“manomayo ca hi te, poṭṭhapāda, attā abhavissa sabbaṅgapaccaṅgī ahīnindriyo,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But with such a mind-made self, Poṭṭhapāda, complete with all its parts, not defective in any sense-organ.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ santampi kho te, poṭṭhapāda, aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In that case, perception would be one thing, and the self another.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tadamināpetaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here is another way to understand how perception and self are different things.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tiṭṭhateva sāyaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, manomayo attā sabbaṅgapaccaṅgī ahīnindriyo,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{As long as that mind-made self persists, complete with all its parts, not defective in any sense-organ,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha imassa purisassa aññā ca saññā uppajjanti, aññā ca saññā nirujjhanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{certain perceptions would arise in a person, and others pass away.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imināpi kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way you can see that perception must be one thing, the self another.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{419.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{23.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“arūpiṃ kho ahaṃ, bhante, attānaṃ paccemi saññāmayan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, I assume a formless self, made up of perception.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“arūpī ca hi te, poṭṭhapāda, attā abhavissa saññāmayo,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But with such a formless self, poṭṭhapāda, made up of perception.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ santampi kho te, poṭṭhapāda, aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In that case, perception would be one thing, and the self another.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tadamināpetaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Here is another way to understand how perception and self are different things.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tiṭṭhateva sāyaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, arūpī attā saññāmayo,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{As long as that formless self persists, made up of perception,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha imassa purisassa aññā ca saññā uppajjanti, aññā ca saññā nirujjhanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{certain perceptions would arise in a person, and others pass away.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imināpi kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, pariyāyena veditabbaṃ yathā aññāva saññā bhavissati añño attā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{In this way you can see that perception must be one thing, the self another.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{420.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sakkā panetaṃ, bhante, mayā ñātuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But Lord, is it possible for me to know whether:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘saññā purisassa attā’ti vā ‘aññāva saññā añño attāti vā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{perception is a person’s self, or whether perception is one thing, and self another?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“dujjānaṃ kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, tayā aññadiṭṭhikena aññakhantikena aññarucikena aññatrāyogena aññatrācariyakena:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhāpada, it is difficult for one of different views, a different faith, under different influences, with different pursuits and a different training to know whether:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘saññā purisassa attā’ti vā, ‘aññāva saññā añño attāti vā’”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{perception is a person’s self, or whether perception is one thing, and self another?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{25.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sace taṃ, bhante, mayā dujjānaṃ aññadiṭṭhikena aññakhantikena aññarucikena aññatrāyogena aññatrācariyakena:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, if this question of self and perceptions is difficult for one of different views, a different faith, under different influences, with different pursuits and a different training to know whether:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘saññā purisassa attā’ti vā, ‘aññāva saññā añño attā’ti vā;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{perception is a person’s self, or whether perception is one thing, and self another?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘kiṃ pana, bhante, sassato loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then, is the world eternal? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{abyākataṃ kho etaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, mayā:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘sassato loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The world is eternal. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘asassato loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, is the world not eternal? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘asassato loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The world is not eternal. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘antavā loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, is the world infinite? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘antavā loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The world is infinite. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘anantavā loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, is the world not infinite? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘anantavā loko, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The world is not infinite. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīraṃ, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, is the soul the same as the body, Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīraṃ, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The soul the same as the body. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīraṃ, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, is the soul one thing and the body another? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīraṃ, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The soul is one thing and the body another. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, does the Tathāgata exists after death? Is only this true and all else false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The Tathāgata exists after death. Only this is true and that the opposite view is false.’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, does the Tathāgata not exist after death? Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The Tathāgata does not exist after death. Only this true and the opposite false?’’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, does the Tathāgata both exist and not exist after death?’ Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The Tathāgata both exists and does not exist after death. Only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, ‘neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Well, Lord, does the Tathāgata neither exist nor not exist after death?’ Is only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etampi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā abyākataṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have not declared,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā, idameva saccaṃ moghamaññan’”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘The Tathāgata neither exists nor does not exist after death. Only this true and the opposite false?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{28.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kasmā panetaṃ, bhante, bhagavatā abyākatan”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But, Lord, why has the Lord not declared these things?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“na hetaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, atthasaṃhitaṃ na dhammasaṃhitaṃ nādibrahmacariyakaṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhāpada, that is not conducive to the purpose, not conducive to Dhamma, not the way to embark on the holy life;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saṃvattati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{it does not lead to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to calm, to higher knowledge, to enlightenment, to Nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā etaṃ mayā abyākatan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is why I have not declared it.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{29.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kiṃ pana, bhante, bhagavatā byākatan”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But, Lord, what has the Lord declared?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“idaṃ dukkhanti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā byākataṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, I have declared: “This is suffering,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhasamudayoti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā byākataṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{this is the origin of suffering,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhanirodhoti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā byākataṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{this is the cessation of suffering,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā byākatan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and this is the path leading to the cessation of suffering.”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kasmā panetaṃ, bhante, bhagavatā byākatan”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But, Lord, why has the Lord declared this?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“etañhi, poṭṭhapāda, atthasaṃhitaṃ, etaṃ dhammasaṃhitaṃ, etaṃ ādibrahmacariyakaṃ,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Because, Poṭṭhapāda, this is conducive to the purpose, conducive to Dhamma, the way to embark on the holy life;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{etaṃ nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṃvattati;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{it leads to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to calm, to higher knowledge, to enlightenment, to Nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā etaṃ mayā byākatan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is why I have declared it.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evametaṃ, bhagavā, evametaṃ, sugata.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘So it is, Lord, so it is, Well-Farer.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yassadāni, bhante, bhagavā kālaṃ maññatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And now is the time for the Blessed Lord to do as he sees fit.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho bhagavā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkāmi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then the Lord rose from his seat and went away.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{421.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{31.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho te paribbājakā acirapakkantassa bhagavato poṭṭhapādaṃ paribbājakaṃ samantato vācā sannitodakena sañjhabbharimakaṃsu:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then the wanderers, as soon as the Lord had left, reproached, sneered and jeered at Poṭṭhapāda from all sides, saying:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evameva panāyaṃ bhavaṃ poṭṭhapādo yaññadeva samaṇo gotamo bhāsati, taṃ tadevassa abbhanumodati:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Whatever the ascetic Gotama says, Poṭṭhapāda agrees with him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘evametaṃ bhagavā evametaṃ, sugatā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“So it is, Lord, so it is, Well-Farer!”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na kho pana mayaṃ kiñci samaṇassa gotamassa ekaṃsikaṃ dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāma:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{We understand that the ascetic Gotama didn’t make any definitive statement at all regarding whether:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘sassato loko’ti vā, ‘asassato loko’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Is the world eternal or not?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘antavā loko’ti vā, ‘anantavā loko’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is it finite or infinite?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīran’ti vā, ‘aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīran’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is the soul the same as the body or different?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā, ‘na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Does the Tathāgata exist after death or not,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā, ‘neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or both, or neither?”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vutte poṭṭhapādo paribbājako te paribbājake etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Poṭṭhapāda replied:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ahampi kho, bho, na kiñci samaṇassa gotamassa ekaṃsikaṃ dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘I too understand that the ascetic Gotama didn’t make any definitive statement at all regarding whether :}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘sassato loko’ti vā, ‘asassato loko’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Is the world eternal or not?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘antavā loko’ti vā, ‘anantavā loko’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is it finite or infinite?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīran’ti vā, ‘aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīran’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is the soul the same as the body or different?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā, ‘na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Does the Tathāgata exist after death or not,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā, ‘neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti vā”ti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or both, or neither?”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{api ca samaṇo gotamo bhūtaṃ tacchaṃ tathaṃ paṭipadaṃ paññapeti dhammaṭṭhitataṃ dhammaniyāmataṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But the ascetic Gotama teaches a true and real way of practice which is consonant with Dhamma and grounded in Dhamma.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhūtaṃ kho pana tacchaṃ tathaṃ paṭipadaṃ paññapentassa dhammaṭṭhitataṃ dhammaniyāmataṃ, kathañhi nāma mādiso viññū samaṇassa gotamassa subhāsitaṃ subhāsitato nābbhanumodeyyā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And why should not a man like me express approval of such a true and real practice, so well taught by the ascetic Gotama?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{422.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{32.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atha kho dvīhatīhassa accayena citto ca hatthisāriputto poṭṭhapādo ca paribbājako yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Two or three days later, Citta, the son of the elephant-trainer, went with Poṭṭhāpada to see the Lord.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{upasaṅkamitvā citto hatthisāriputto bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Citta prostrated himself before the Lord and sat down to one side.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{poṭṭhapādo pana paribbājako bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Potthapada exchanged courtesies with the Lord, sat down to one side,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Having exchanged courtesies and greetings,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ekamantaṃ nisinno kho poṭṭhapādo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Potthapada sat to the side and told him what had happened:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tadā maṃ, bhante, te paribbājakā acirapakkantassa bhagavato samantato vācāsannitodakena sañjhabbharimakaṃsu:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{"the wanderers, as soon as the Lord had left, reproached, sneered and jeered me from all sides, saying:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘evameva panāyaṃ bhavaṃ poṭṭhapādo yaññadeva samaṇo gotamo bhāsati, taṃ tadevassa abbhanumodati:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Whatever the ascetic Gotama says, Poṭṭhapāda agrees with him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘evametaṃ bhagavā evametaṃ sugatā”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“So it is, Lord, so it is, Well-Farer!”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na kho pana mayaṃ kiñci samaṇassa gotamassa ekaṃsikaṃ dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāma:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{We understand that the ascetic Gotama didn’t make any definitive statement at all regarding whether:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sassato loko”ti vā, “asassato loko”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Is the world eternal or not?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“antavā loko”ti vā, “anantavā loko”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is it finite or infinite?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīran”ti vā, “aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīran”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is the soul the same as the body or different?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā, “na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Does the Tathāgata exist after death or not,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā, “neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or both, or neither?”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vuttāhaṃ, bhante, te paribbājake etadavocaṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then I replied:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ahampi kho, bho, na kiñci samaṇassa gotamassa ekaṃsikaṃ dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘I too understand that the ascetic Gotama didn’t make any definitive statement at all regarding whether :}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sassato loko”ti vā, “asassato loko”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Is the world eternal or not?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“antavā loko”ti vā, “anantavā loko”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is it finite or infinite?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīran”ti vā, “aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīran”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Is the soul the same as the body or different?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā, “na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{— Does the Tathāgata exist after death or not,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā, “neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā”ti vā;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or both, or neither?”’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{api ca samaṇo gotamo bhūtaṃ tacchaṃ tathaṃ paṭipadaṃ paññapeti dhammaṭṭhitataṃ dhammaniyāmataṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But the ascetic Gotama teaches a true and real way of practice which is consonant with Dhamma and grounded in Dhamma.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhūtaṃ kho pana tacchaṃ tathaṃ paṭipadaṃ paññapentassa dhammaṭṭhitataṃ dhammaniyāmataṃ, kathañhi nāma mādiso viññū samaṇassa gotamassa subhāsitaṃ subhāsitato nābbhanumodeyyā”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And why should not a man like me express approval of such a true and real practice, so well taught by the ascetic Gotama?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{423.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sabbeva kho ete, poṭṭhapāda, paribbājakā andhā acakkhukā; tvaṃyeva nesaṃ eko cakkhumā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, all those wanderers are blind and sightless, you alone among them are sighted.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ekaṃsikāpi hi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā dhammā desitā paññattā;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Some things I have taught and pointed out, Poṭṭhāpada, as being certain,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{anekaṃsikāpi hi kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā dhammā desitā paññattā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And other things I have taught and pointed out, Poṭṭhāpada, as being uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“katame ca te, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Which are the things I have pointed out as uncertain?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘sassato loko’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The world is eternal.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘asassato loko’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The world is not eternal.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘antavā loko’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The world is infinite.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘anantavā loko’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The world is not infinite.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīran’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The soul the same as the body.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīran’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The soul is one thing and the body another.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The Tathāgata exists after death.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The Tathāgata does not exist after death.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘hoti ca na ca hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The Tathāgata both exists and does not exist after death.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘neva hoti na na hoti tathāgato paraṃ maraṇā’ti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“The Tathāgata neither exists nor does not exist after death.”, I have declared to be uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kasmā ca te, poṭṭhapāda, mayā anekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Why have I declared them to be uncertain?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na hete, poṭṭhapāda, atthasaṃhitā na dhammasaṃhitā na ādibrahmacariyakā}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because they are not conducive to the purpose, not conducive to Dhamma, not the way to embark on the holy life;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na nibbidāya na virāgāya na nirodhāya na upasamāya na abhiññāya na sambodhāya na nibbānāya saṃvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{it does not lead to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to calm, to higher knowledge, to enlightenment, to Nibbāna.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā te mayā anekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā”.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is why I have declared them as uncertain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{424.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“katame ca te, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But what things have I pointed out as certain?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{idaṃ dukkhanti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“This is suffering, I have declared to be certain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhasamudayoti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the origin of suffering, I have declared to be certain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhanirodhoti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the cessation of suffering, I have declared to be certain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti kho, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsiko dhammo desito paññatto.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{This is the path leading to the cessation of suffering, I have declared to be certain.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“kasmā ca te, poṭṭhapāda, mayā ekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Why have I declared to them as certain?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ete, poṭṭhapāda, atthasaṃhitā, ete dhammasaṃhitā, ete ādibrahmacariyakā}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Because they are conducive to the purpose, conducive to Dhamma, the way to embark on the holy life;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ete nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya upasamāya abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṃvattanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{they lead to disenchantment, to dispassion, to cessation, to calm, to higher knowledge, to enlightenment, to Nibbana.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tasmā te mayā ekaṃsikā dhammā desitā paññattā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is why I have declared them as certain.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{425.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{34.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“santi, poṭṭhapāda, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā evaṃvādino evaṃdiṭṭhino:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, there are some ascetics and Brahmins who declare this doctrin and view:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ekantasukhī attā hoti arogo paraṃ maraṇā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘After death, the self is entirely happy and free from disease.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tyāhaṃ upasaṅkamitvā evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I approached them and asked}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and they replied: “Yes.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tyāhaṃ evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\

\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto ekaṃ vā rattiṃ ekaṃ vā divasaṃ upaḍḍhaṃ vā rattiṃ upaḍḍhaṃ vā divasaṃ ekantasukhiṃ attānaṃ sañjānāthā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto yā tā devatā ekantasukhaṃ lokaṃ upapannā, tāsaṃ bhāsamānānaṃ saddaṃ suṇātha:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Such being the case, does not the talk of those ascetics and Brahmins turn out to be stupid?}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{426.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Well, as to this most beautiful girl in the country,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\setstretch{.7}

\end{addmargin}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ambho purisa, yassa tvaṃ pāsādassa ārohaṇāya nisseṇiṃ karosi,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Well now, this staircase for a palace that you are building;}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{jānāsi taṃ pāsādaṃ puratthimāya vā disāya dakkhiṇāya vā disāya pacchimāya vā disāya uttarāya vā disāya ucco vā nīco vā majjhimo vā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{do you know whether the palace will face east, or west, or north or south, or whether it will be high, low or of medium height?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭho ‘no’ti vadeyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and he would say: “No.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tamenaṃ evaṃ vadeyyuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And they might say:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ambho purisa, yaṃ tvaṃ na jānāsi na passasi, tassa tvaṃ pāsādassa ārohaṇāya nisseṇiṃ karosī’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Well then, you don’t know or see what kind of a palace you are building the staircase for?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭho ‘āmā’ti vadeyya.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Asked this, he’d say, ‘Yes.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ kiṃ maññasi, poṭṭhapāda, nanu evaṃ sante tassa purisassa appāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Don’t you think that man’s talk would turn out to be stupid?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“addhā kho, bhante, evaṃ sante tassa purisassa appāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Certainly, Lord.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{36.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā evaṃvādino evaṃdiṭṭhino:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘And so it is, Poṭṭhapāda, with those same ascetics and Brahmins who declare this doctrin and view:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ekantasukhī attā hoti arogo paraṃ maraṇā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘After death, the self is entirely happy and free from disease.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tyāhaṃ upasaṅkamitvā evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I approached them and asked}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘saccaṃ kira tumhe āyasmanto evaṃvādino evaṃdiṭṭhino:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{if this was indeed what they declared and believed,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“ekantasukhī attā hoti arogo paraṃ maraṇā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘After death, the self is entirely happy and free from disease.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{te ce me evaṃ puṭṭhā ‘āmā’ti paṭijānanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and they replied: “Yes.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tyāhaṃ evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Then I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto ekantasukhaṃ lokaṃ jānaṃ passaṃ viharathā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Do you, friends, living in the world, know and see it as an entirely happy place?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭhā ‘no’ti vadanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and they replied: “No.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tyāhaṃ evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto ekaṃ vā rattiṃ ekaṃ vā divasaṃ upaḍḍhaṃ vā rattiṃ upaḍḍhaṃ vā divasaṃ ekantasukhiṃ attānaṃ sañjānāthā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Have you ever experienced a single night or day, or half a night or day, that was entirely happy?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭhā ‘no’ti vadanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and they replied: “No.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tyāhaṃ evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto jānātha}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Do you know:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{ayaṃ maggo ayaṃ paṭipadā ekantasukhassa lokassa sacchikiriyāyā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{a path or a practice whereby an entirely happy world might be brought about?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭhā ‘no’ti vadanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and they replied: “No.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tyāhaṃ evaṃ vadāmi:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{I said:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘api pana tumhe āyasmanto yā tā devatā ekantasukhaṃ lokaṃ upapannā’, tāsaṃ devatānaṃ bhāsamānānaṃ saddaṃ suṇātha:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Have you heard the voices of deities who have been reborn in an entirely happy world, saying:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“suppaṭipannāttha, mārisā, ujuppaṭipannāttha, mārisā, ekantasukhassa lokassa sacchikiriyāya;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Practice well, dear sirs, practice directly so as to realize an exclusively happy world.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mayampi hi, mārisā, evaṃpaṭipannā ekantasukhaṃ lokaṃ upapannā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{For this is how we practiced, and we were reborn in an exclusively happy world”?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{iti puṭṭhā “no”ti vadanti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Asked this, they replied: “No.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ kiṃ maññasi, poṭṭhapāda,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What do you think, Poṭṭhapāda?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{nanu evaṃ sante tesaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ appāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Such being the case, does not the talk of those ascetics and Brahmins turn out to be stupid?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“addhā kho, bhante, evaṃ sante tesaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ appāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Clearly that’s the case, sir, the talk of those ascetics and Brahmins turn out to be stupid.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{428.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{39.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“tayo kho me, poṭṭhapāda, attapaṭilābhā - oḷāriko attapaṭilābho, manomayo attapaṭilābho, arūpo attapaṭilābho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Poṭṭhapāda, there are three kinds of “acquired self”: the gross acquired self, the mind-made acquired self, the formless acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo ca, poṭṭhapāda, oḷāriko attapaṭilābho?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What is the gross acquired self?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{rūpī cātumahābhūtiko kabaḷīkārāhārabhakkho, ayaṃ oḷāriko attapaṭilābho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It has form, is composed of the four great elements, nourished by material food.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo manomayo attapaṭilābho?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What is the mind-made self?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{rūpī manomayo sabbaṅgapaccaṅgī ahīnindriyo, ayaṃ manomayo attapaṭilābho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It has form, complete with all its parts, not defective in any sense-organ.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{katamo arūpo attapaṭilābho?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{What is the formless acquired self?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{arūpī saññāmayo, ayaṃ arūpo attapaṭilābho.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is without form, and made up of perception.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{429.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{40.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“oḷārikassapi kho ahaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, attapaṭilābhassa pahānāya dhammaṃ desemi -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘But I teach a doctrine for getting rid of the gross acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yathāpaṭipannānaṃ vo saṃkilesikā dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{whereby defiling mental states disappear}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and states tending to purification grow strong,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paññāpāripūriṃ vepullattañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissathāti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{siyā kho pana te, poṭṭhapāda, evamassa -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Now, Poṭṭhāpada, you might think:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saṃkilesikā dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Perhaps these defiling mental states might disappear}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and states tending to purification grow strong,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paññāpāripūriṃ vepullattañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{dukkho ca kho vihāroti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one might still be unhappy.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na kho panetaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, evaṃ daṭṭhabbaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{That is not how it should be regarded.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saṃkilesikā ceva dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{If defiling states disappear}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā ca dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and states tending to purification grow strong,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paññāpāripūriṃ vepullattañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pāmujjaṃ ceva bhavissati pīti ca passaddhi ca sati ca sampajaññañca sukho ca vihāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{nothing but happiness and delight develops, tranquillity, mindfulness and clear awareness — and that is a happy state.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{430.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{41.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“manomayassapi kho ahaṃ, poṭṭhapāda, attapaṭilābhassa pahānāya dhammaṃ desemi -}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{saṃkilesikā ceva dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{If defiling states disappear}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā ca dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and states tending to purification grow strong,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paññāpāripūriṃ vepullattañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{pāmujjaṃ ceva bhavissati pīti ca passaddhi ca sati ca sampajaññañca sukho ca vihāro.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{nothing but happiness and delight develops, tranquillity, mindfulness and clear awareness — and that is a happy state.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{431.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{42.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘I also teach a doctrine for getting rid of the formless acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
