\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one might still be unhappy.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}

\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Certainly, Lord.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{435.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{46.}}\\
\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“seyyathāpi, poṭṭhapāda, puriso nisseṇiṃ kareyya pāsādassa ārohaṇāya tasseva pāsādassa heṭṭhā.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘It is just as if a man were to build a staircase for a palace, which was below that palace.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tamenaṃ evaṃ vadeyyuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{They might say to him:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ambho purisa, yassa tvaṃ pāsādassa ārohaṇāya nisseṇiṃ karosi,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Well now, this staircase for a palace that you are building,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{jānāsi taṃ pāsādaṃ, puratthimāya vā disāya dakkhiṇāya vā disāya pacchimāya vā disāya uttarāya vā}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{do you know whether the palace will face east or west, or north or south,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{disāya ucco vā nīco vā majjhimo vā’ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or whether it will be high, low or of medium height?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{so evaṃ vadeyya:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and he would say:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ayaṃ vā so, āvuso, pāsādo, yassāhaṃ ārohaṇāya nisseṇiṃ karomi, tasseva pāsādassa heṭṭhā’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“This staircase is right under the palace.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ kiṃ maññasi, poṭṭhapāda, nanu evaṃ sante tassa purisassa sappāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Don’t you think that man’s statement would be well-founded?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“addhā kho, bhante, evaṃ sante tassa purisassa sappāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Certainly, Lord.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{436.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

{\EnglishColumn{47.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“evameva kho, poṭṭhapāda, pare ce amhe evaṃ puccheyyuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘katamo pana so, āvuso, oḷāriko attapaṭilābho, yassa tumhe pahānāya dhammaṃ desetha,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“What is this gross acquired self whose abandonment you preach,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yathāpaṭipannānaṃ vo saṃkilesikā dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{whereby defiling mental states disappear}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{vodāniyā dhammā abhivaḍḍhissanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and states tending to purification grow strong,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paññāpāripūriṃ vepullattañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissathā’ti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tesaṃ mayaṃ evaṃ puṭṭhā evaṃ byākareyyāma:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{being so asked, we should reply:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ayaṃ vā so, āvuso, arūpo attapaṭilābho, yassa mayaṃ pahānāya dhammaṃ desema,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“This is this gross acquired self for the getting rid of which we teach a doctrine,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yathāpaṭipannānaṃ vo saṃkilesikā dhammā pahīyissanti,}}\\

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{and one gains and remains in the purity and perfection of wisdom here and now, having realised and attained it by one’s own super-knowledge.”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“taṃ kiṃ maññasi, poṭṭhapāda, nanu evaṃ sante sappāṭihīrakataṃ bhāsitaṃ sampajjatī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Don’t you think that statement is well-founded?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Certainly, Lord.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

{\EnglishColumn{48.}}\\

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vutte citto hatthisāriputto bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{At this, Citta, son of the elephant-trainer, said to the Lord:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yasmiṃ, bhante, samaye oḷāriko attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, whenever the gross acquired self is present,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{moghassa tasmiṃ samaye manomayo attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{would it be wrong to assume the existence of the mind-made acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{mogho arūpo attapaṭilābho hoti;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or of the formless acquired self?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{oḷāriko vāssa attapaṭilābho tasmiṃ samaye sacco hoti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Does only the gross acquired self truly exist then?}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ, bhante, samaye manomayo attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\

\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“yasmiṃ, citta, samaye oḷāriko attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\

\end{addmargin}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{438.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sace taṃ, citta, evaṃ puccheyyuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Citta, suppose they were to ask you:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ahosi tvaṃ atītamaddhānaṃ, na tvaṃ nāhosi;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{“Did you exist in the past or didn’t you,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{bhavissasi tvaṃ anāgatamaddhānaṃ, na tvaṃ na bhavissasi;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{will you exist in the future or won’t you,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{atthi tvaṃ etarahi, na tvaṃ natthī’ti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{do you exist now or don’t you?”}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ puṭṭho tvaṃ, citta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{how would you answer?’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“sace maṃ, bhante, evaṃ puccheyyuṃ:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Lord, if I were asked:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘ahosi tvaṃ atītamaddhānaṃ, na tvaṃ na ahosi;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}

\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{    -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{53.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evameva kho, citta, yasmiṃ samaye oḷāriko attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘So too, whenever the gross acquired self is present,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{neva tasmiṃ samaye manomayo attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not at that time speak of a mind-made acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na arūpo attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not speak of a formless acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{oḷāriko attapaṭilābho tveva tasmiṃ samaye saṅkhaṃ gacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{We speak only of a gross acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ, citta, samaye manomayo attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Whenever the mind-made acquired self is present,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{neva tasmiṃ samaye oḷāriko attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not at that time speak of a gross acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na arūpo attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not speak of a formless acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{manomayo attapaṭilābho tveva tasmiṃ samaye saṅkhaṃ gacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{We speak only of a mind-made acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yasmiṃ, citta, samaye arūpo attapaṭilābho hoti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Whenever the formless acquired self is present,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{neva tasmiṃ samaye oḷāriko attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not at that time speak of a gross acquired self,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{na manomayo attapaṭilābhoti saṅkhaṃ gacchati;}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{we do not speak of a mind-made acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{arūpo attapaṭilābho tveva tasmiṃ samaye saṅkhaṃ gacchati.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{We speak only of a formless acquired self.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{imā kho citta, lokasamaññā lokaniruttiyo lokavohārā lokapaññattiyo, yāhi tathāgato voharati aparāmasan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But, Citta, these are merely names, expressions, turns of speech, designations in common use in the world, which the Tathāgata uses without misapprehending them.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{441.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{54.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evaṃ vutte, poṭṭhapādo paribbājako bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And at these words Poṭṭhapāda the wanderer said to the Lord:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“abhikkantaṃ, bhante! abhikkantaṃ, bhante!}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Excellent, Lord, excellent!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, bhante, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is as if someone were to set up what had been knocked down,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or to point out the way to one who had got lost,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya: ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or to bring an oil-lamp into a dark place, so that those with eyes could see what was there.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṃ bhagavatā anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Just so the Blessed Lord has expounded the Dhamma in various ways.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{esāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavantaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Lord, I go for refuge to the Lord, the Dhamma and the Sangha.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{upāsakaṃ maṃ bhagavā dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gatan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{May the Lord accept me as a lay-follower who has taken refuge in him from this day forth as long as life shall last!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{442.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{55.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{citto pana hatthisāriputto bhagavantaṃ etadavoca:}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{But Citta, son of the elephant-trainer, said to the Lord:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{“abhikkantaṃ, bhante; abhikkantaṃ, bhante!}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Excellent, Lord, excellent!}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{seyyathāpi, bhante, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{It is as if someone were to set up what had been knocked down,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or to point out the way to one who had got lost,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya: ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{or to bring an oil-lamp into a dark place, so that those with eyes could see what was there.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{evamevaṃ bhagavatā anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Just so the Blessed Lord has expounded the Dhamma in various ways.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{esāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavantaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{Lord, I go for refuge to the Lord, the Dhamma and the Sangha.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{labheyyāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampadan”ti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{May I, Lord, receive the going-forth at the Lord’s hands, may I receive ordination!’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{443.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{56.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{alattha kho citto hatthisāriputto bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And Citta, son of the elephant-trainer, received the going-forth at the Lord’s hands, and the ordination.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{acirūpasampanno kho panāyasmā citto hatthisāriputto eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto na cirasseva -}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And the newly-ordained Venerable Citta, alone, secluded, unwearying, zealous and resolute, in a short time}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti,}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{attained to that for the sake of which young men of good birth go forth from the household life into homelessness,}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{tadanuttaraṃ - brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{that unexcelled culmination of the holy life, having realised it here and now by his own super-knowledge and dwelt therein, knowing:}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ, nāparaṃ itthattāyā’ti - abbhaññāsi.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{‘Birth is destroyed, the holy life has been lived, what had to be done has been done, there is nothing further here.’}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{aññataro kho panāyasmā citto hatthisāriputto arahataṃ ahosīti.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{And the Venerable Citta, son of the elephant-trainer, became another of the Arahants.}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}

\vskip 0.05in
\begin{absolutelynopagebreak}
\setstretch{.7}
{\PaliColumn{poṭṭhapādasuttaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ navamaṃ.}}\\
\begin{addmargin}[1em]{2em}
\setstretch{.5}
{\EnglishColumn{    -}}\\
\end{addmargin}
\end{absolutelynopagebreak}
